[Running Redis with TLS](#running-redis-with-tls)\\n- [Code contributions](#code-contributions)\\n- [Redis Trademarks](#redis-trademarks)\\n\\n## What is Redis?\\n\\nFor developers, who are building real-time data-driven applications, Redis is the preferred, fastest, and most feature-rich cache, data structure server, and document and vector query engine.\\n\\n### Key use cases\\n\\nRedis excels in various applications, including:\\n\\n- **Caching:** Supports multiple eviction policies, key expiration, and hash-field expiration.\\n- **Distributed Session Store:** Offers flexible session data modeling (string, JSON, hash).\\n- **Data Structure Server:** Provides low-level data structures (strings, lists, sets, hashes, sorted sets, JSON, etc.) with high-level semantics (counters, queues, leaderboards, rate limiters) and supports transactions & scripting.\\n- **NoSQL Data Store:** Key-value, document, and time series data storage.\\n- **Search and Query Engine:** Indexing for hash/JSON documents, supporting vector search, full-text search, geospatial queries, ranking, and aggregations via Redis Search.\\n- **Event Store & Message Broker:** Implements queues (lists), priority queues (sorted sets), event deduplication (sets), streams, and pub/sub with probabilistic stream processing capabilities.\\n- **Vector Store for GenAI:** Integrates with AI applications (e.g. LangGraph, mem0) for short-term memory, long-term memory, LLM response caching (semantic caching), and retrieval augmented generation (RAG).\\n- **Real-Time Analytics:** Powers personalization, recommendations, fraud detection, and risk assessment.\\n\\n## Why choose Redis?\\n\\nRedis is a popular choice for developers worldwide due to its combination of speed, flexibility, and rich feature set. Here's why people choose Redis for:\\n\\n- **Performance:** Because Redis keeps data primarily in memory and uses efficient data structures, it achieves extremely low latency (often sub-millisecond) for both read and write operations. This makes it ideal for applications demanding real-time responsiveness.\\n- **Flexibility:** Redis isn't just a key-value store, it provides native support for a wide range of data structures and capabilities listed in [What is Redis?](#what-is-redis)\\n- **Extensibility:** Redis is not limited to the built-in data structures, it has a [modules API](https://redis.io/docs/latest/develop/reference/modules/) that makes it possible to extend Redis functionality and rapidly implement new Redis commands\\n- **Simplicity:** Redis has a simple, text-based protocol and [well-documented command set](https://redis.io/docs/latest/commands/)\\n- **Ubiquity:** Redis is battle tested in production workloads at a massive scale. There is a good chance you indirectly interact with Redis several times daily\\n- **Versatility**: Redis is the de facto standard for use cases such as:\\n  - **Caching:** quickly access frequently used data without needing to query your primary database\\n  - **Session management:** read and write user session data without hurting user experience or slowing down every API call\\n  - **Querying, sorting, and analytics:** perform deduplication, full text search, and secondary indexing on in-memory data as fast as possible\\n  - **Messaging and interservice communication:** job queues, message brokering, pub/sub, and streams for communicating between services\\n  - **Vector operations:** Long-term and short-term LLM memory, RAG content retrieval, semantic caching, semantic routing, and vector similarity search\\n\\nIn summary, Redis provides a powerful, fast, and flexible toolkit for solving a wide variety of data management challenges. If you want to know more, here is a list of starting points:\\n\\n- [**Introduction to Redis data types**](https://redis.io/docs/latest/develop/data-types/)\\n- [**The full list of Redis commands**](https://redis.io/commands/)\\n- [**Redis for AI**](https://redis.io/docs/latest/develop/ai/)\\n- [**Redis documentation**](https://redis.io/documentation/)\\n\\n## What is Redis Open Source?\\n\\nRedis Community Edition (Redis CE) was renamed Redis Open Source with the v8.0 release.\\n\\nRedis Ltd. also offers [Redis Software](https://redis.io/enterprise/), a self-managed software with additional compliance, reliability, and resiliency for enterprise scaling,\\nand [Redis Cloud](https://redis.io/cloud/), a fully managed service integrated with Google Cloud, Azure, and AWS for production-ready apps.\\n\\nRead more about the differences between Redis Open Source and Redis [here](https:/...[truncated]","startedAt":null,"finishedAt":"2026-06-10T05:25:13.079239302Z","errorCode":null,"message":"SUCCEEDED"}}

[Running Redis with TLS](#running-redis-with-tls)\\n- [Code contributions](#code-contributions)\\n- [Redis Trademarks](#redis-trademarks)\\n\\n## What is Redis?\\n\\nFor developers, who are building real-time data-driven applications, Redis is the preferred, fastest, and most feature-rich cache, data structure server, and document and vector query engine.\\n\\n### Key use cases\\n\\nRedis excels in various applications, including:\\n\\n- **Caching:** Supports multiple eviction policies, key expiration, and hash-field expiration.\\n- **Distributed Session Store:** Offers flexible session data modeling (string, JSON, hash).\\n- **Data Structure Server:** Provides low-level data structures (strings, lists, sets, hashes, sorted sets, JSON, etc.) with high-level semantics (counters, queues, leaderboards, rate limiters) and supports transactions & scripting.\\n- **NoSQL Data Store:** Key-value, document, and time series data storage.\\n- **Search and Query Engine:** Indexing for hash/JSON documents, supporting vector search, full-text search, geospatial queries, ranking, and aggregations via Redis Search.\\n- **Event Store & Message Broker:** Implements queues (lists), priority queues (sorted sets), event deduplication (sets), streams, and pub/sub with probabilistic stream processing capabilities.\\n- **Vector Store for GenAI:** Integrates with AI applications (e.g. LangGraph, mem0) for short-term memory, long-term memory, LLM response caching (semantic caching), and retrieval augmented generation (RAG).\\n- **Real-Time Analytics:** Powers personalization, recommendations, fraud detection, and risk assessment.\\n\\n## Why choose Redis?\\n\\nRedis is a popular choice for developers worldwide due to its combination of speed, flexibility, and rich feature set. Here's why people choose Redis for:\\n\\n- **Performance:** Because Redis keeps data primarily in memory and uses efficient data structures, it achieves extremely low latency (often sub-millisecond) for both read and write operations. This makes it ideal for applications demanding real-time responsiveness.\\n- **Flexibility:** Redis isn't just a key-value store, it provides native support for a wide range of data structures and capabilities listed in [What is Redis?](#what-is-redis)\\n- **Extensibility:** Redis is not limited to the built-in data structures, it has a [modules API](https://redis.io/docs/latest/develop/reference/modules/) that makes it possible to extend Redis functionality and rapidly implement new Redis commands\\n- **Simplicity:** Redis has a simple, text-based protocol and [well-documented command set](https://redis.io/docs/latest/commands/)\\n- **Ubiquity:** Redis is battle tested in production workloads at a massive scale. There is a good chance you indirectly interact with Redis several times daily\\n- **Versatility**: Redis is the de facto standard for use cases such as:\\n  - **Caching:** quickly access frequently used data without needing to query your primary database\\n  - **Session management:** read and write user session data without hurting user experience or slowing down every API call\\n  - **Querying, sorting, and analytics:** perform deduplication, full text search, and secondary indexing on in-memory data as fast as possible\\n  - **Messaging and interservice communication:** job queues, message brokering, pub/sub, and streams for communicating between services\\n  - **Vector operations:** Long-term and short-term LLM memory, RAG content retrieval, semantic caching, semantic routing, and vector similarity search\\n\\nIn summary, Redis provides a powerful, fast, and flexible toolkit for solving a wide variety of data management challenges. [Running Redis with TLS](#running-redis-with-tls)\\n- [Code contributions](#code-contributions)\\n- [Redis Trademarks](#redis-trademarks)\\n\\n## What is Redis?\\n\\nFor developers, who are building real-time data-driven applications, Redis is the preferred, fastest, and most feature-rich cache, data structure server, and document and vector query engine.\\n\\n### Key use cases\\n\\nRedis excels in various applications, including:\\n\\n- **Caching:** Supports multiple eviction policies, key expiration, and hash-field expiration.\\n- **Distributed Session Store:** Offers flexible session data modeling (string, JSON, hash).\\n- **Data Structure Server:** Provides low-level data structures (strings, lists, sets, hashes, sorted sets, JSON, etc.) with high-level semantics (counters, queues, leaderboards, rate limiters) and supports transactions & scripting.\\n- **NoSQL Data Store:** Key-value, document, and time series data storage.\\n- **Search and Query Engine:** Indexing for hash/JSON documents, supporting vector search, full-text search, geospatial queries, ranking, and aggregations via Redis Search.\\n- **Event Store & Message Broker:** Implements queues (lists), priority queues (sorted sets), event deduplication (sets), streams, and pub/sub with probabilistic stream processing capabilities.\\n- **Vector Store for GenAI:** Integrates with AI applications (e.g. LangGraph, mem0) for short-term memory, long-term memory, LLM response caching (semantic caching), and retrieval augmented generation (RAG).\\n- **Real-Time Analytics:** Powers personalization, recommendations, fraud detection, and risk assessment.\\n\\n## Why choose Redis?\\n\\nRedis is a popular choice for developers worldwide due to its combination of speed, flexibility, and rich feature set. Here's why people choose Redis for:\\n\\n- **Performance:** Because Redis keeps data primarily in memory and uses efficient data structures, it achieves extremely low latency (often sub-millisecond) for both read and write operations. This makes it ideal for applications demanding real-time responsiveness.\\n- **Flexibility:** Redis isn't just a key-value store, it provides native support for a wide range of data structures and capabilities listed in [What is Redis?](#what-is-redis)\\n- **Extensibility:** Redis is not limited to the built-in data structures, it has a [modules API](https://redis.io/docs/latest/develop/reference/modules/) that makes it possible to extend Redis functionality and rapidly implement new Redis commands\\n- **Simplicity:** Redis has a simple, text-based protocol and [well-documented command set](https://redis.io/docs/latest/commands/)\\n- **Ubiquity:** Redis is battle tested in production workloads at a massive scale. There is a good chance you indirectly interact with Redis several times daily\\n- **Versatility**: Redis is the de facto standard for use cases such as:\\n  - **Caching:** quickly access frequently used data without needing to query your primary database\\n  - **Session management:** read and write user session data without hurting user experience or slowing down every API call\\n  - **Querying, sorting, and analytics:** perform deduplication, full text search, and secondary indexing on in-memory data as fast as possible\\n  - **Messaging and interservice communication:** job queues, message brokering, pub/sub, and streams for communicating between services\\n  - **Vector operations:** Long-term and short-term LLM memory, RAG content retrieval, semantic caching, semantic routing, and vector similarity search\\n\\nIn summary, Redis provides a powerful, fast, and flexible toolkit for solving a wide variety of data management challenges. If you want to know more, here is a list of starting points:\\n\\n- [**Introduction to Redis data types**](https://redis.io/docs/latest/develop/data-types/)\\n- [**The full list of Redis commands**](https://redis.io/commands/)\\n- [**Redis for AI**](https://redis.io/docs/latest/develop/ai/)\\n- [**Redis documentation**](https://redis.io/documentation/)\\n\\n## What is Redis Open Source?\\n\\nRedis Community Edition (Redis CE) was renamed Redis Open Source with the v8.0 release.\\n\\nRedis Ltd. also offers [Redis Software](https://redis.io/enterprise/), a self-managed software with additional compliance, reliability, and resiliency for enterprise scaling,\\nand [Redis Cloud](https://redis.io/cloud/), a fully managed service integrated with Google Cloud, Azure, and AWS for production-ready apps.\\n\\nRead more about the differences between Redis Open Source and Redis [here](https:/...[truncated]","startedAt":null,"finishedAt":"2026-06-10T05:25:22.212859195Z","errorCode":null,"message":"SUCCEEDED"}}

[Running Redis with TLS](#running-redis-with-tls)\\n- [Code contributions](#code-contributions)\\n- [Redis Trademarks](#redis-trademarks)\\n\\n## What is Redis?\\n\\nFor developers, who are building real-time data-driven applications, Redis is the preferred, fastest, and most feature-rich cache, data structure server, and document and vector query engine.\\n\\n### Key use cases\\n\\nRedis excels in various applications, including:\\n\\n- **Caching:** Supports multiple eviction policies, key expiration, and hash-field expiration.\\n- **Distributed Session Store:** Offers flexible session data modeling (string, JSON, hash).\\n- **Data Structure Server:** Provides low-level data structures (strings, lists, sets, hashes, sorted sets, JSON, etc.) with high-level semantics (counters, queues, leaderboards, rate limiters) and supports transactions & scripting.\\n- **NoSQL Data Store:** Key-value, document, and time series data storage.\\n- **Search and Query Engine:** Indexing for hash/JSON documents, supporting vector search, full-text search, geospatial queries, ranking, and aggregations via Redis Search.\\n- **Event Store & Message Broker:** Implements queues (lists), priority queues (sorted sets), event deduplication (sets), streams, and pub/sub with probabilistic stream processing capabilities.\\n- **Vector Store for GenAI:** Integrates with AI applications (e.g. LangGraph, mem0) for short-term memory, long-term memory, LLM response caching (semantic caching), and retrieval augmented generation (RAG).\\n- **Real-Time Analytics:** Powers personalization, recommendations, fraud detection, and risk assessment.\\n\\n## Why choose Redis?\\n\\nRedis is a popular choice for developers worldwide due to its combination of speed, flexibility, and rich feature set. Here's why people choose Redis for:\\n\\n- **Performance:** Because Redis keeps data primarily in memory and uses efficient data structures, it achieves extremely low latency (often sub-millisecond) for both read and write operations. There is a good chance you indirectly interact with Redis several times daily\\n- **Versatility**: Redis is the de facto standard for use cases such as:\\n  - **Caching:** quickly access frequently used data without needing to query your primary database\\n  - **Session management:** read and write user session data without hurting user experience or slowing down every API call\\n  - **Querying, sorting, and analytics:** perform deduplication, full text search, and secondary indexing on in-memory data as fast as possible\\n  - **Messaging and interservice communication:** job queues, message brokering, pub/sub, and streams for communicating between services\\n  - **Vector operations:** Long-term and short-term LLM memory, RAG content retrieval, semantic caching, semantic routing, and vector similarity search\\n\\nIn summary, Redis provides a powerful, fast, and flexible toolkit for solving a wide variety of data management challenges. The background features subtle circuit board patterns and binary code, with a clean, professional blue and white color scheme.\\n\\n---\\n\\n# Slide 2: Redis 核心定位与数据结构\\n\\n**Title:** Redis 是什么？核心数据结构概览\\n\\n**Key Bullets:**\\n*   **定义**：高性能、开源的内存数据结构服务器。\\n*   **基础结构**：String, Hash, List, Set, Sorted Set。\\n*   **高级结构**：JSON (RedisJSON), Stream (Redis Streams)。\\n*   **优势**：单线程事件循环模型带来的极低延迟。\\n\\n**Speaker Notes:**\\nRedis 本质上是一个内存数据结构存储。它支持丰富的数据类型，从基础的 String 到复杂的 JSON 和 Stream。这些数据结构直接映射到应用层，减少了序列化/反序列化的开销。其核心优势在于基于 C 语言编写的事件循环模型，使得它在处理高并发请求时具有极高的吞吐量。\\n\\n**Image Prompt:**\\nAn infographic displaying various Redis data structures (String, Hash, List, Set, Sorted Set, JSON, Stream) as distinct, colorful icons arranged in a circular flow, symbolizing versatility and speed.\\n\\n---\\n\\n# Slide 3: 核心架构与通信协议\\n\\n**Title:** 底层架构：事件驱动与 RESP 协议\\n\\n**Key Bullets:**\\n*   **语言**：C 语言编写，极致性能。\\n*   **模型**：单线程事件循环 (Event Loop) 处理命令。\\n*   **协议**：RESP (Redis Serialization Protocol)。\\n*   **特点**：简单、轻量、易于解析，支持管道化操作。\\n\\n**Speaker Notes:**\\nRedis 的架构核心在于其单线程事件循环模型，这避免了多线程上下文切换的开销。客户端与服务器之间通过 RESP 协议通信，这是一种简单且高效的文本协议。这种设计使得 Redis 能够以极低的延迟处理数百万次每秒的操作。\\n\\n**Image Prompt:**\\nA technical diagram showing a single thread processing multiple client requests via an event loop, connected to a database memory block. The connection line is labeled \\\"RESP Protocol\\\", highlighting the simplicity and efficiency of the communication.\\n\\n---\\n\\n# Slide 4: 持久化机制\\n\\n**Title:** 数据安全：RDB 与 AOF 持久化\\n\\n**Key Bullets:**\\n*   **RDB (Redis Database)**：\\n    *   在指定时间间隔内生成数据集的时间点快照。\\n    *   适合大规模数据恢复，文件紧凑。\\n*   **AOF (Append Only File)**：\\n    *   以日志形式记录每个写操作。\\n    *   数据安全性更高，支持多种同步策略 (always/everysec/no)。\\n*   **混合持久化**：结合两者优势。\\n\\n**Speaker Notes:**\\n内存数据面临断电丢失的风险，因此持久化至关重要。Redis 提供 RDB 和 AOF 两种机制。RDB 适合备份和灾难恢复，而 AOF 则能提供更细粒度的数据保护。现代 Redis 版本支持混合持久化，既保留了 RDB 的快速加载优势，又具备 AOF 的高安全性。\\n\\n**Image Prompt:**\\nA split-screen illustration: on the left, a snapshot of data being compressed into a file (RDB), on the right, a continuous log file growing as data is written (AOF). A shield icon overlays both, symbolizing data protection.\\n\\n---\\n\\n# Slide 5: 高可用与集群方案\\n\\n**Title:** 高可用架构：复制、哨兵与集群\\n\\n**Key Bullets:**\\n*   **主从复制 (Master-Slave)**：实现数据冗余和读写分离。\\n*   **Redis Sentinel**：\\n    *   监控主从节点。\\n    *   自动故障转移 (Failover)。\\n*   **Redis Cluster**：\\n    *   去中心化分布式架构。\\n    *   数据分片 (Sharding) 与自动故障转移。\\n    *   支持水平扩展。\\n\\n**Speaker Notes:**\\n在生产环境中，高可用性是必须的。Redis 提供了三种主要方案：主从复制用于基础冗余；Sentinel 用于监控和自动故障转移；而 Redis Cluster 则通过数据分片实现了真正的分布式存储和水平扩展，能够处理 PB 级数据和千万级 QPS。\\n\\n**Image Prompt:**\\nA network topology diagram showing a central Master node connected to multiple Slave nodes. Sentinel nodes are shown monitoring the Master. A second diagram shows a Cluster with multiple Master-Slave pairs interconnected, representing distributed sharding.\\n\\n---\\n\\n# Slide 6: 官方模块扩展机制\\n\\n**Title:** 模块化扩展：Modules API 与官方模块\\n\\n**Key Bullets:**\\n*   **Modules API**：允许使用 C 或 Rust 编写自定义模块，扩展 Redis 功能。\\n*   **RedisSearch**：\\n    *   全文搜索、向量搜索、地理空间搜索。\\n    *   无需外部搜索引擎。\\n*   **RedisJSON**：\\n    *   原生支持 JSON 文档存储与查询。\\n*   **RedisAI**：\\n    *   在 Redis 内存中运行机器学习模型推理。\\n\\n**Speaker Notes:**\\nRedis 的强大之处在于其可扩展性。通过 Modules API，开发者可以扩展 Redis 的功能。官方提供的 RedisSearch 让我们能在内存中进行复杂的全文和向量搜索；RedisJSON 支持原生 JSON 操作；而 RedisAI 则允许直接在数据库层执行模型推理，减少了数据移动。\\n\\n**Image Prompt:**\\nA modular puzzle piece design where the central piece is the Redis logo, surrounded by interlocking pieces labeled \\\"Search\\\", \\\"JSON\\\", \\\"AI\\\", and \\\"Graph\\\", representing the extensible module ecosystem.\\n\\n---\\n\\n# Slide 7: 消息队列与事件驱动\\n\\n**Title:** 实时通信：Streams 与 Pub/Sub\\n\\n**Key Bullets:**\\n*   **Redis Streams**：\\n    *   持久化的消息队列。\\n    *   支持消费者组 (Consumer Groups) 和消息确认。\\n    *   类似 Kafka 的轻量级替代方案。\\n*   **Pub/Sub**：\\n    *   发布/订阅模式。\\n    *   实时广播，但消息不持久化（无确认机制）。\\n*   **应用场景**：实时通知、日志聚合、聊天室。\\n\\n**Speaker Notes:**\\n除了数据存储，Redis 也是优秀的消息中间件。Redis Streams 提供了持久化、可回溯的消息队列，支持消费者组模式，非常适合实时数据处理。而 Pub/Sub 则适用于简单的实时广播场景，如即时通知系统。\\n\\n**Image Prompt:**\\nA visual representation of data packets flowing from a publisher to multiple subscribers. One path shows a persistent log (Streams), and another shows a broadcast wave (Pub/Sub), illustrating real-time data distribution.\\n\\n---\\n\\n# Slide 8: AI 时代的新角色：向量存储\\n\\n**Title:** GenAI 赋能：Redis 作为向量数据库\\n\\n**Key Bullets:**\\n*   **向量存储 (Vector Storage)**：\\n    *   支持存储高维向量数据。\\n    *   集成 RedisSearch 的向量索引 (HNSW, FLAT)。\\n*   **语义搜索**：\\n    *   基于向量相似度 (Cosine, L2) 进行检索。\\n    *   结合全文搜索实现混合检索 (Hybrid Search)。\\n*   **RAG 架构核心**：\\n    *   快速检索上下文，减少 LLM 幻觉。\\n    *   低延迟向量相似度计算。\\n\\n**Speaker Notes:**\\n在 AI 时代，Redis 成为了构建 RAG (检索增强生成) 应用的关键组件。通过 RedisSearch 的向量索引功能，Redis 可以高效存储和检索嵌入向量 (Embeddings)。这使得应用能够快速从海量数据中检索相关上下文，显著提升大语言模型的回答准确性和实时性。\\n\\n**Image Prompt:**\\nA neural network visualization where nodes are connected by lines representing vector similarities. The connection line is labeled \\\"RESP Protocol\\\", highlighting the simplicity and efficiency of the communication.\\n\\n---\\n\\n# Slide 4: 持久化机制\\n\\n**Title:** 数据安全：RDB 与 AOF 持久化\\n\\n**Key Bullets:**\\n*   **RDB (Redis Database)**：\\n    *   在指定时间间隔内生成数据集的时间点快照。\\n    *   适合大规模数据恢复，文件紧凑。\\n*   **AOF (Append Only File)**：\\n    *   以日志形式记录每个写操作。\\n    *   数据安全性更高，支持多种同步策略 (always/everysec/no)。\\n*   **混合持久化**：结合两者优势。\\n\\n**Speaker Notes:**\\n内存数据面临断电丢失的风险，因此持久化至关重要。Redis 提供 RDB 和 AOF 两种机制。RDB 适合备份和灾难恢复，而 AOF 则能提供更细粒度的数据保护。现代 Redis 版本支持混合持久化，既保留了 RDB 的快速加载优势，又具备 AOF 的高安全性。\\n\\n**Image Prompt:**\\nA split-screen illustration: on the left, a snapshot of data being compressed into a file (RDB), on the right, a continuous log file growing as data is written (AOF). event:stream_event
data:{"eventId":"322970749941174272","eventSeq":"1056","eventType":"STEP_FINISHED","runId":"run_322969346103431168","stepId":null,"timestamp":"2026-06-10T05:30:27.292074617Z","typedPayload":{"runId":"run_322969346103431168","stepId":"model-turn-13","stepNo":13,"stepType":"MODEL_TURN","status":"SUCCEEDED","title":"Model turn","summary":null,"startedAt":"2026-06-10T05:28:38.364689348Z","finishedAt":"2026-06-10T05:30:27.290450029Z","durationMs":"108925","errorCode":null,"message":"所有硬性工具已成功调用完毕。现在生成最终中文 Markdown项目介绍。\n\n---\n\n# Redis开源项目图文介绍\n\n# # 一、项目概览Redis（Remote Dictionary Server）是一个开源的、高性能的**内存数据结构服务器**，被广泛用作缓存、数据库、消息代理和向量搜索引擎。该项目由 Salvatore Sanfilippo（antirez）于2009年创建，目前由 Redis Ltd.维护，是全球最流行的实时数据平台之一。根据 GitHub仓库 README的描述，Redis 的定位是：\"For developers, who are building real-time data-driven applications, Redis is the preferred, fastest, and most feature-rich cache, data structure server, and document and vector query engine.\"（对于构建实时数据驱动应用的开发者而言，Redis是首选的、最快的、功能最丰富的缓存、数据结构服务器以及文档和向量查询引擎。）Redis的核心特点包括：\n- **极致性能**：数据主要驻留内存，使用高效的数据结构，读写延迟通常低于1毫秒。\n- **丰富的数据结构**：原生支持 String、Hash、List、Set、Sorted Set、JSON、Stream、Bitmap、HyperLogLog、Geo等。\n- **持久化机制**：支持 RDB快照和 AOF追加日志两种持久化方式，以及两者的混合持久化。\n- **高可用与分布式**：提供主从复制、Redis Sentinel（哨兵）和 Redis Cluster（集群）三种高可用方案。\n- **模块化扩展**：通过 Modules API支持以 C/Rust编写自定义模块，官方提供 RedisSearch、RedisJSON、RedisAI等模块。\n- **AI时代的新角色**：支持向量存储和向量搜索，成为 RAG（检索增强生成）和 GenAI应用的关键基础设施。\n\n## 二、架构设计\n\n### 2.1整体架构分层Redis的架构可以分为以下核心层次：\n\n```mermaid\nflowchart TD\nsubgraph\nClient[客户端层]\nC1[Redis CLI]\nC2[Python Client]\nC3[Java/Jedis]\nC4[Go Client]\nC5[Node.js/ioredis]\nC6[Redis Insight]\nend\nsubgraph\nProtocol[协议层]\nP1[RESP协议解析]\nP2[管道/PubSub/事务]\nend\nsubgraph\nCore[核心引擎层]\nE1[命令执行引擎]\nE2[内存管理]\nE3[事件循环]\nE4[持久化模块]\nend\nsubgraph\nDataStructures[数据结构层]\nD1[String]\nD2[Hash]\nD3[List]\nD4[Set]\nD5[Sorted Set]\nD6[JSON]\nD7[Stream]\nD8[Bitmap/HyperLogLog/Geo]\nend\nsubgraph\nPersistence[持久化层]\nS1[RDB快照]\nS2[AOF追加日志]\nS3[混合持久化]\nend\nsubgraph\nCluster[集群层]\nCL1[主从复制]\nCL2[Redis Sentinel]\nCL3[Redis Cluster]\nend\nsubgraph\nExtensions[扩展层]\nM1[Redis Modules API]\nM2[RedisSearch]\nM3[RedisJSON]\nM4[RedisAI]\nM5[RedisGraph]\nend %% Connections C1 & C2 & C3 & C4 & C5 &\nC6 --> P1\nP1 --> P2\nP2 --> E1\nE1 --> E2\nE1 --> E3\nE1 --> E4\nE2 --> D1 & D2 & D3 & D4 & D5 & D6 & D7 & D8\nE4 --> S1 & S2 & S3\nE3 --> CL1\nCL1 --> CL2\nCL2 --> CL3\nM1 --> M2 & M3 & M4 & M5 M2 & M3 & M4 &\nM5 -.-> **核心引擎层**：采用单线程事件循环模型，包含命令执行引擎、内存管理、事件循环和持久化模块。\n- **数据结构层**：提供8种以上的原生数据结构，每种数据结构都有对应的底层编码（如 SDS、skiplist、ziplist等）。\n- **持久化层**：RDB提供时间点快照，AOF提供操作日志，混合持久化结合两者优势。\n- **集群层**：主从复制实现数据冗余，Sentinel实现自动故障转移，Cluster实现分布式分片和水平扩展。\n- **扩展层**：通过 Modules API支持官方和社区模块的扩展，包括搜索、JSON、AI、图数据库等功能。\n\n## 三、架构图\n\n```mermaid\nflowchart Markdown项目介绍。\n\n---\n\n# Redis开源项目图文介绍\n\n# # 一、项目概览Redis（Remote Dictionary Server）是一个开源的、高性能的**内存数据结构服务器**，被广泛用作缓存、数据库、消息代理和向量搜索引擎。该项目由 Salvatore Sanfilippo（antirez）于2009年创建，目前由 Redis Ltd.维护，是全球最流行的实时数据平台之一。根据 GitHub仓库 README的描述，Redis 的定位是：\"For developers, who are building real-time data-driven applications, Redis is the preferred, fastest, and most feature-rich cache, data structure server, and document and vector query engine.\"（对于构建实时数据驱动应用的开发者而言，Redis是首选的、最快的、功能最丰富的缓存、数据结构服务器以及文档和向量查询引擎。）Redis的核心特点包括：\n- **极致性能**：数据主要驻留内存，使用高效的数据结构，读写延迟通常低于1毫秒。\n- **丰富的数据结构**：原生支持 String、Hash、List、Set、Sorted Set、JSON、Stream、Bitmap、HyperLogLog、Geo等。\n- **持久化机制**：支持 RDB快照和 AOF追加日志两种持久化方式，以及两者的混合持久化。\n- **高可用与分布式**：提供主从复制、Redis Sentinel（哨兵）和 Redis Cluster（集群）三种高可用方案。\n- **模块化扩展**：通过 Modules API支持以 C/Rust编写自定义模块，官方提供 RedisSearch、RedisJSON、RedisAI等模块。\n- **AI时代的新角色**：支持向量存储和向量搜索，成为 RAG（检索增强生成）和 GenAI应用的关键基础设施。\n\n## 二、架构设计\n\n###
